**Based on work by Martín Escardó.**

Preliminaries
=============

We assume a fixed frame `F` on which to define the frame of nuclei.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="729" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="736" href="PatchFrame.html" class="Module">PatchFrame</a> <a id="747" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="748" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="750" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="752" href="Frame.html#3701" class="Function">Frame</a> <a id="758" href="Basis.html#3042" class="Generalizable">𝒰</a> <a id="760" href="Basis.html#3044" class="Generalizable">𝒱</a> <a id="762" href="Basis.html#3046" class="Generalizable">𝒲</a><a id="763" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="765" class="Keyword">where</a>
</pre>
<pre class="Agda"><a id="784" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="789" href="Poset.html#3652" class="Module">PosetReasoning</a> <a id="804" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="805" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="809" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a><a id="810" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="812" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="818" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="819" href="Poset.html#3694" class="Function Operator">_⊑⟨_⟩_</a><a id="825" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="827" href="Poset.html#3832" class="Function Operator">_■</a><a id="829" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
For simplicity, we will refer to the order, the meet, and the join of `F` simply
as `⊑`, _⊓_`, and `⋁_`.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="_⊑_"></a><a id="950" href="PatchFrame.html#950" class="Function Operator">_⊑_</a> <a id="954" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="956" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="958" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="960" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="963" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="965" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="967" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="969" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="972" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="974" href="Cubical.Foundations.HLevels.html#1500" class="Function">hProp</a> <a id="980" href="PatchFrame.html#760" class="Bound">𝒱</a>
<a id="982" href="PatchFrame.html#982" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="984" href="PatchFrame.html#950" class="Function Operator">⊑</a> <a id="986" href="PatchFrame.html#986" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="988" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="990" href="PatchFrame.html#982" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="992" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">⊑[</a> <a id="995" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="999" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1001" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">]</a> <a id="1003" href="PatchFrame.html#986" class="Bound">y</a>

<a id="_⊓_"></a><a id="1006" href="PatchFrame.html#1006" class="Function Operator">_⊓_</a> <a id="1010" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1012" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="1014" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1016" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="1019" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1021" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="1023" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1025" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="1028" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1030" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="1032" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1034" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a>
<a id="1037" href="PatchFrame.html#1037" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="1039" href="PatchFrame.html#1006" class="Function Operator">⊓</a> <a id="1041" href="PatchFrame.html#1041" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="1043" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1045" href="PatchFrame.html#1037" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="1047" href="Frame.html#4167" class="Function">⊓[</a> <a id="1050" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1052" href="Frame.html#4167" class="Function">]</a> <a id="1054" href="PatchFrame.html#1041" class="Bound">y</a>

<a id="⋁_"></a><a id="1057" href="PatchFrame.html#1057" class="Function Operator">⋁_</a> <a id="1060" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1062" href="Basis.html#5634" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="1066" href="PatchFrame.html#762" class="Bound">𝒲</a> <a id="1068" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="1070" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1072" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="1075" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1077" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="1079" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1081" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a>
<a id="1084" href="PatchFrame.html#1057" class="Function Operator">⋁</a> <a id="1086" href="PatchFrame.html#1086" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="1088" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1090" href="Frame.html#4300" class="Function Operator">⋁[</a> <a id="1093" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1095" href="Frame.html#4300" class="Function Operator">]</a> <a id="1097" href="PatchFrame.html#1086" class="Bound">U</a>
</pre>
We define the notion of Scott-continuity of a nucleus on `F` as follows:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="isScottCont′"></a><a id="1186" href="PatchFrame.html#1186" class="Function">isScottCont′</a> <a id="1199" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1201" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1202" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="1204" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1206" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="1209" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1211" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="1213" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1215" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a><a id="1217" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1219" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1221" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1222" href="PatchFrame.html#758" class="Bound">𝒰</a> <a id="1224" href="Basis.html#3075" class="Function Operator">∨</a> <a id="1226" href="PatchFrame.html#760" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="1228" href="Basis.html#3075" class="Function Operator">∨</a> <a id="1230" href="PatchFrame.html#762" class="Bound">𝒲</a> <a id="1232" href="Basis.html#3138" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="1233" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1235" href="Basis.html#3184" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="1237" href="PatchFrame.html#1186" class="Function">isScottCont′</a> <a id="1250" href="PatchFrame.html#1250" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="1252" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="1256" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1257" href="PatchFrame.html#1257" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="1259" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1261" href="Basis.html#5634" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="1265" href="PatchFrame.html#762" class="Bound">𝒲</a> <a id="1267" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="1269" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1271" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a><a id="1273" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1275" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="1281" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="1283" href="Poset.html#7416" class="Function">isDirected</a> <a id="1294" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1295" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="1299" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a><a id="1300" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1302" href="PatchFrame.html#1257" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="1304" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">]</a> <a id="1306" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1308" href="PatchFrame.html#1250" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="1310" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1311" href="PatchFrame.html#1057" class="Function Operator">⋁</a> <a id="1313" href="PatchFrame.html#1257" class="Bound">U</a><a id="1314" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1316" href="Agda.Builtin.Cubical.Path.html#381" class="Function Operator">≡</a> <a id="1318" href="Frame.html#4300" class="Function Operator">⋁[</a> <a id="1321" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1323" href="Frame.html#4300" class="Function Operator">]</a> <a id="1325" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">⁅</a> <a id="1327" href="PatchFrame.html#1250" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="1329" href="PatchFrame.html#1333" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="1331" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">∣</a> <a id="1333" href="PatchFrame.html#1333" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="1335" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">ε</a> <a id="1337" href="PatchFrame.html#1257" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="1339" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">⁆</a>

<a id="isScottCont"></a><a id="1342" href="PatchFrame.html#1342" class="Function">isScottCont</a> <a id="1354" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1356" href="Nucleus.html#601" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="1364" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1366" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1368" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1369" href="PatchFrame.html#758" class="Bound">𝒰</a> <a id="1371" href="Basis.html#3075" class="Function Operator">∨</a> <a id="1373" href="PatchFrame.html#760" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="1375" href="Basis.html#3075" class="Function Operator">∨</a> <a id="1377" href="PatchFrame.html#762" class="Bound">𝒲</a> <a id="1379" href="Basis.html#3138" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="1380" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1382" href="Basis.html#3184" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="1384" href="PatchFrame.html#1342" class="Function">isScottCont</a> <a id="1396" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1397" href="PatchFrame.html#1397" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="1399" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="1401" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="1404" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1406" href="PatchFrame.html#1186" class="Function">isScottCont′</a> <a id="1419" href="PatchFrame.html#1397" class="Bound">j</a>
</pre>
The type expression the notion of being Scott-continuous is an h-proposition
as one would expect:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="isScottCont-prop"></a><a id="1533" href="PatchFrame.html#1533" class="Function">isScottCont-prop</a> <a id="1550" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1552" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1553" href="PatchFrame.html#1553" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="1555" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1557" href="Nucleus.html#601" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="1565" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a><a id="1566" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1568" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1570" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#10148" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="1577" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1578" href="PatchFrame.html#1342" class="Function">isScottCont</a> <a id="1590" href="PatchFrame.html#1553" class="Bound">𝒿</a><a id="1591" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="1593" href="PatchFrame.html#1533" class="Function">isScottCont-prop</a> <a id="1610" href="PatchFrame.html#1610" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="1612" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="1616" href="Cubical.Foundations.HLevels.html#14996" class="Function">isPropΠ</a> <a id="1624" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="1626" href="PatchFrame.html#1626" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="1628" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1630" href="Cubical.Foundations.HLevels.html#14996" class="Function">isPropΠ</a> <a id="1638" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="1640" href="PatchFrame.html#1640" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="1642" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1644" href="Poset.html#3444" class="Function">carrier-is-set</a> <a id="1659" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1660" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="1664" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a><a id="1665" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1667" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="1669" class="Symbol">_</a>
</pre>
We define a shorthand for the type of Scott-continuous nuclei as we will be
primarily interested in those:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="ScottContNucleus"></a><a id="1792" href="PatchFrame.html#1792" class="Function">ScottContNucleus</a> <a id="1809" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1811" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1812" href="PatchFrame.html#758" class="Bound">𝒰</a> <a id="1814" href="Basis.html#3075" class="Function Operator">∨</a> <a id="1816" href="PatchFrame.html#760" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="1818" href="Basis.html#3075" class="Function Operator">∨</a> <a id="1820" href="PatchFrame.html#762" class="Bound">𝒲</a> <a id="1822" href="Basis.html#3138" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="1823" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1825" href="Basis.html#3184" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="1827" href="PatchFrame.html#1792" class="Function">ScottContNucleus</a> <a id="1844" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1846" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">Σ[</a> <a id="1849" href="PatchFrame.html#1849" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="1851" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">∈</a> <a id="1853" href="Nucleus.html#601" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="1861" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="1863" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">]</a> <a id="1865" href="PatchFrame.html#1342" class="Function">isScottCont</a> <a id="1877" href="PatchFrame.html#1849" class="Bound">j</a>

<a id="ScottContNucleus-set"></a><a id="1880" href="PatchFrame.html#1880" class="Function">ScottContNucleus-set</a> <a id="1901" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1903" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#10203" class="Function">isSet</a> <a id="1909" href="PatchFrame.html#1792" class="Function">ScottContNucleus</a>
<a id="1926" href="PatchFrame.html#1880" class="Function">ScottContNucleus-set</a> <a id="1947" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="1951" href="Cubical.Foundations.HLevels.html#12444" class="Function">isSetΣ</a> <a id="1958" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1959" href="Nucleus.html#1482" class="Function">Nucleus-set</a> <a id="1971" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a><a id="1972" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1974" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1975" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#13767" class="Function">isProp→isSet</a> <a id="1988" href="Cubical.Foundations.Function.html#402" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="1990" href="PatchFrame.html#1533" class="Function">isScottCont-prop</a><a id="2006" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="ScottContNucleus-eq"></a><a id="2009" href="PatchFrame.html#2009" class="Function">ScottContNucleus-eq</a> <a id="2029" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2031" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2032" href="PatchFrame.html#2032" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="2034" href="PatchFrame.html#2034" class="Bound">𝓀</a> <a id="2036" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2038" href="PatchFrame.html#1792" class="Function">ScottContNucleus</a><a id="2054" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2056" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2058" href="PatchFrame.html#2032" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="2060" class="Symbol">.</a><a id="2061" href="PatchFrame.html#549" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="2065" class="Symbol">.</a><a id="2066" href="PatchFrame.html#549" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="2070" href="Agda.Builtin.Cubical.Path.html#381" class="Function Operator">≡</a> <a id="2072" href="PatchFrame.html#2034" class="Bound">𝓀</a> <a id="2074" class="Symbol">.</a><a id="2075" href="PatchFrame.html#549" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="2079" class="Symbol">.</a><a id="2080" href="PatchFrame.html#549" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="2084" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2086" href="PatchFrame.html#2032" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="2088" href="Agda.Builtin.Cubical.Path.html#381" class="Function Operator">≡</a> <a id="2090" href="PatchFrame.html#2034" class="Bound">𝓀</a>
<a id="2092" href="PatchFrame.html#2009" class="Function">ScottContNucleus-eq</a> <a id="2112" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="2114" href="PatchFrame.html#2114" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="2116" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="2118" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="2121" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="2123" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="2126" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="2128" href="PatchFrame.html#2128" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="2130" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="2132" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="2135" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="2137" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="2140" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="2144" href="Cubical.Data.Sigma.Properties.html#11948" class="Function">Σ≡Prop</a> <a id="2151" href="PatchFrame.html#1533" class="Function">isScottCont-prop</a> <a id="2168" href="Cubical.Foundations.Function.html#402" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="2170" href="Cubical.Data.Sigma.Properties.html#11948" class="Function">Σ≡Prop</a> <a id="2177" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2178" href="Nucleus.html#1070" class="Function">isNuclear-prop</a> <a id="2193" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a><a id="2194" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
Poset of nuclei on `F` (`𝔑`)
============================

The set of endofunctions on a given frame forms a poset under the pointwise
order; we denote by `_⊑f_` this pointwise order and by `𝔉` this poset.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="_⊑f_"></a><a id="2416" href="PatchFrame.html#2416" class="Function Operator">_⊑f_</a> <a id="2421" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2423" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2424" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="2426" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="2428" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="2431" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2433" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="2435" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="2437" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a><a id="2439" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2441" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2443" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2444" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="2446" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="2448" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="2451" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2453" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="2455" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="2457" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a><a id="2459" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2461" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2463" href="Cubical.Foundations.HLevels.html#1500" class="Function">hProp</a> <a id="2469" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2470" href="PatchFrame.html#758" class="Bound">𝒰</a> <a id="2472" href="Basis.html#3075" class="Function Operator">∨</a> <a id="2474" href="PatchFrame.html#760" class="Bound">𝒱</a><a id="2475" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="2477" href="PatchFrame.html#2477" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="2479" href="PatchFrame.html#2416" class="Function Operator">⊑f</a> <a id="2482" href="PatchFrame.html#2482" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="2484" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2486" href="Cubical.Functions.Logic.html#4500" class="Function">∀[</a> <a id="2489" href="PatchFrame.html#2489" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="2491" href="Cubical.Functions.Logic.html#4500" class="Function">∶</a> <a id="2493" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="2495" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="2497" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="2500" href="Cubical.Functions.Logic.html#4500" class="Function">]</a> <a id="2502" href="PatchFrame.html#2477" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="2504" href="PatchFrame.html#2489" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="2506" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">⊑[</a> <a id="2509" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="2513" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="2515" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">]</a> <a id="2517" href="PatchFrame.html#2482" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="2519" href="PatchFrame.html#2489" class="Bound">x</a>

<a id="⊑f-refl"></a><a id="2522" href="PatchFrame.html#2522" class="Function">⊑f-refl</a> <a id="2530" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2532" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="2534" href="Poset.html#469" class="Function">isReflexive</a> <a id="2546" href="PatchFrame.html#2416" class="Function Operator">_⊑f_</a> <a id="2551" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">]</a>
<a id="2553" href="PatchFrame.html#2522" class="Function">⊑f-refl</a> <a id="2561" href="PatchFrame.html#2561" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="2563" href="PatchFrame.html#2563" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="2565" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2567" href="Poset.html#3014" class="Function Operator">⊑[</a> <a id="2570" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="2574" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="2576" href="Poset.html#3014" class="Function Operator">]-refl</a> <a id="2583" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2584" href="PatchFrame.html#2561" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="2586" href="PatchFrame.html#2563" class="Bound">x</a><a id="2587" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="2913" href="PatchFrame.html#2893" class="Function">𝔉</a> <a id="2915" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2917" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2918" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="2920" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="2922" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="2925" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2927" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="2929" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="2931" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a><a id="2933" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2935" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="2937" href="PatchFrame.html#2416" class="Function Operator">_⊑f_</a> <a id="2942" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="2944" href="PatchFrame.html#2687" class="Function">is-set</a> <a id="2951" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="2953" href="PatchFrame.html#2522" class="Function">⊑f-refl</a> <a id="2961" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="2963" href="PatchFrame.html#2590" class="Function">⊑f-trans</a> <a id="2972" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="2974" href="PatchFrame.html#2766" class="Function">⊑f-antisym</a>

<a id="_∙∧∙_"></a><a id="2986" href="PatchFrame.html#2986" class="Function Operator">_∙∧∙_</a> <a id="2992" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2994" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2995" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="2997" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="2999" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="3002" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3004" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="3006" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="3008" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a><a id="3010" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3012" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3014" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3015" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="3017" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="3019" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="3022" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3024" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="3026" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="3028" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a><a id="3030" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3032" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3034" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="3036" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="3038" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="3041" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3043" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="3045" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="3047" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a>
<a id="3050" href="PatchFrame.html#3050" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="3052" href="PatchFrame.html#2986" class="Function Operator">∙∧∙</a> <a id="3056" href="PatchFrame.html#3056" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="3058" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3060" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="3062" href="PatchFrame.html#3062" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="3064" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3066" href="PatchFrame.html#3050" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="3068" href="PatchFrame.html#3062" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="3070" href="Frame.html#4167" class="Function">⊓[</a> <a id="3073" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="3075" href="Frame.html#4167" class="Function">]</a> <a id="3077" href="PatchFrame.html#3056" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="3079" href="PatchFrame.html#3062" class="Bound">x</a>
</pre>
We denote by `𝔑` the poset of nuclei:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="𝔑"></a><a id="3133" href="PatchFrame.html#3133" class="Function">𝔑</a> <a id="3135" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3137" href="Poset.html#2165" class="Function">Poset</a> <a id="3143" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3144" href="PatchFrame.html#758" class="Bound">𝒰</a> <a id="3146" href="Basis.html#3075" class="Function Operator">∨</a> <a id="3148" href="PatchFrame.html#760" class="Bound">𝒱</a><a id="3149" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3151" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3152" href="PatchFrame.html#758" class="Bound">𝒰</a> <a id="3154" href="Basis.html#3075" class="Function Operator">∨</a> <a id="3156" href="PatchFrame.html#760" class="Bound">𝒱</a><a id="3157" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="3159" href="PatchFrame.html#549" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="3163" href="PatchFrame.html#3133" class="Function">𝔑</a> <a id="3165" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3167" href="Nucleus.html#601" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="3175" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a>
<a id="3177" href="PatchFrame.html#560" class="Field">snd</a> <a id="3181" href="PatchFrame.html#3133" class="Function">𝔑</a> <a id="3183" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3185" href="PatchFrame.html#3201" class="Function">𝔑-str</a>
  <a id="3193" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="3201" href="PatchFrame.html#3201" class="Function">𝔑-str</a> <a id="3207" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3209" href="Poset.html#1701" class="Function">PosetStr</a> <a id="3218" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3219" href="PatchFrame.html#758" class="Bound">𝒰</a> <a id="3221" href="Basis.html#3075" class="Function Operator">∨</a> <a id="3223" href="PatchFrame.html#760" class="Bound">𝒱</a><a id="3224" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3226" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3227" href="Nucleus.html#601" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="3235" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a><a id="3236" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="3240" href="PatchFrame.html#3201" class="Function">𝔑-str</a> <a id="3246" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3248" href="PatchFrame.html#3321" class="Function Operator">_⊑n_</a> <a id="3253" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="3255" href="Nucleus.html#1482" class="Function">Nucleus-set</a> <a id="3267" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="3269" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="3271" href="PatchFrame.html#2522" class="Function">⊑f-refl</a> <a id="3279" href="Cubical.Foundations.Function.html#402" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="3281" href="PatchFrame.html#549" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="3285" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="3287" href="PatchFrame.html#3391" class="Function">⊑-trans</a> <a id="3295" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="3297" href="PatchFrame.html#3497" class="Function">⊑-antisym</a>
    <a id="3311" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="3321" href="PatchFrame.html#3321" class="Function Operator">_⊑n_</a> <a id="3326" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3328" href="Poset.html#275" class="Function">Order</a> <a id="3334" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3335" href="PatchFrame.html#758" class="Bound">𝒰</a> <a id="3337" href="Basis.html#3075" class="Function Operator">∨</a> <a id="3339" href="PatchFrame.html#760" class="Bound">𝒱</a><a id="3340" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3342" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3343" href="Nucleus.html#601" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="3351" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a><a id="3352" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="6729" href="PatchFrame.html#6729" class="Function">⦅𝟒⦆</a> <a id="6733" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6735" href="Frame.html#15407" class="Function">cleft</a>  <a id="6742" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="6744" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="6746" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6747" href="Frame.html#4893" class="Function Operator">⊓[</a> <a id="6750" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="6752" href="Frame.html#4893" class="Function Operator">]-lower₀</a> <a id="6761" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6762" href="PatchFrame.html#5317" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="6764" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6765" href="PatchFrame.html#5317" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="6767" href="PatchFrame.html#6228" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6768" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="6771" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6772" href="PatchFrame.html#5317" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="6774" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6775" href="PatchFrame.html#5347" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6777" href="PatchFrame.html#6228" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6778" class="Symbol">)))</a>
    <a id="6786" href="PatchFrame.html#6786" class="Function">⦅𝟓⦆</a> <a id="6790" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6792" href="Frame.html#15407" class="Function">cleft</a>  <a id="6799" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="6801" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="6803" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6804" href="PatchFrame.html#5335" class="Bound">j-n₂</a> <a id="6809" href="PatchFrame.html#6228" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6810" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="6816" href="PatchFrame.html#6816" class="Function">⦅𝟔⦆</a> <a id="6820" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6822" href="Frame.html#15049" class="Function">cright</a> <a id="6829" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="6831" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="6833" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6834" href="PatchFrame.html#5365" class="Bound">k-n₂</a> <a id="6839" href="PatchFrame.html#6228" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6840" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
We now prove that `_⊓n_` is a greatest lower bound operator as expected:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="⊓n-meet"></a><a id="6929" href="PatchFrame.html#6929" class="Function">⊓n-meet</a> <a id="6937" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6939" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="6941" href="Frame.html#1300" class="Function">isGLB</a> <a id="6947" href="PatchFrame.html#3133" class="Function">𝔑</a> <a id="6949" href="PatchFrame.html#5273" class="Function Operator">_⊓n_</a> <a id="6954" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">]</a>
<a id="6956" href="PatchFrame.html#6929" class="Function">⊓n-meet</a> <a id="6964" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6966" href="PatchFrame.html#6990" class="Function">lb</a> <a id="6969" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="6971" href="PatchFrame.html#7157" class="Function">greatest</a>
  <a id="6982" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="6990" href="PatchFrame.html#6990" class="Function">lb</a> <a id="6993" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6995" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6996" href="PatchFrame.html#6996" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="6998" href="PatchFrame.html#6998" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7000" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7002" href="Nucleus.html#601" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="7010" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a><a id="7011" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7013" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7015" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="7017" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7018" href="PatchFrame.html#6996" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="7020" href="PatchFrame.html#5273" class="Function Operator">⊓n</a> <a id="7023" href="PatchFrame.html#6998" class="Bound">k</a><a id="7024" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7026" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">⊑[</a> <a id="7029" href="PatchFrame.html#3133" class="Function">𝔑</a> <a id="7031" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">]</a> <a id="7033" href="PatchFrame.html#6996" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="7035" href="PatchFrame.html#538" class="Function Operator">∧</a> <a id="7037" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7038" href="PatchFrame.html#6996" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="7040" href="PatchFrame.html#5273" class="Function Operator">⊓n</a> <a id="7043" href="PatchFrame.html#6998" class="Bound">k</a><a id="7044" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7046" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">⊑[</a> <a id="7049" href="PatchFrame.html#3133" class="Function">𝔑</a> <a id="7051" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">]</a> <a id="7053" href="PatchFrame.html#6998" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7055" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">]</a>
  <a id="7059" href="PatchFrame.html#6990" class="Function">lb</a> <a id="7062" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7063" href="PatchFrame.html#7063" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="7065" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7067" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="7070" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7071" href="PatchFrame.html#7071" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7073" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7075" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="7078" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="7084" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="7087" href="PatchFrame.html#7087" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7089" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7091" href="Frame.html#4893" class="Function Operator">⊓[</a> <a id="7094" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="7096" href="Frame.html#4893" class="Function Operator">]-lower₀</a> <a id="7105" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7106" href="PatchFrame.html#7063" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="7108" href="PatchFrame.html#7087" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7109" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7111" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7112" href="PatchFrame.html#7071" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7114" href="PatchFrame.html#7087" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7115" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="7118" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7120" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="7123" href="PatchFrame.html#7123" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7125" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7127" href="Frame.html#5023" class="Function Operator">⊓[</a> <a id="7130" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="7132" href="Frame.html#5023" class="Function Operator">]-lower₁</a> <a id="7141" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7142" href="PatchFrame.html#7063" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="7144" href="PatchFrame.html#7123" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7145" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7147" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7148" href="PatchFrame.html#7071" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7150" href="PatchFrame.html#7123" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7151" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="7157" href="PatchFrame.html#7157" class="Function">greatest</a> <a id="7166" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7168" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7169" href="PatchFrame.html#7169" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="7171" href="PatchFrame.html#7171" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7173" href="PatchFrame.html#7173" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="7175" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7177" href="Nucleus.html#601" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="7185" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a><a id="7186" class="Symbol">)</a>
           <a id="7199" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7201" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="7203" href="PatchFrame.html#7173" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="7205" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">⊑[</a> <a id="7208" href="PatchFrame.html#3133" class="Function">𝔑</a> <a id="7210" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">]</a> <a id="7212" href="PatchFrame.html#7169" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="7214" href="PatchFrame.html#538" class="Function Operator">∧</a> <a id="7216" href="PatchFrame.html#7173" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="7218" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">⊑[</a> <a id="7221" href="PatchFrame.html#3133" class="Function">𝔑</a> <a id="7223" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">]</a> <a id="7225" href="PatchFrame.html#7171" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7227" href="Cubical.Functions.Logic.html#1956" class="Function Operator">⇒</a> <a id="7229" href="PatchFrame.html#7173" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="7231" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">⊑[</a> <a id="7234" href="PatchFrame.html#3133" class="Function">𝔑</a> <a id="7236" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">]</a> <a id="7238" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7239" href="PatchFrame.html#7169" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="7241" href="PatchFrame.html#5273" class="Function Operator">⊓n</a> <a id="7244" href="PatchFrame.html#7171" class="Bound">k</a><a id="7245" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7247" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">]</a>
  <a id="7251" href="PatchFrame.html#7157" class="Function">greatest</a> <a id="7260" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7261" href="PatchFrame.html#7261" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="7263" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7265" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="7268" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7269" href="PatchFrame.html#7269" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7271" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7273" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="7276" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7277" href="PatchFrame.html#7277" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="7279" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7281" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="7284" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7285" href="PatchFrame.html#7285" class="Bound">l⊑j</a> <a id="7289" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7291" href="PatchFrame.html#7291" class="Bound">l⊑k</a><a id="7294" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7296" href="PatchFrame.html#7296" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7298" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="7304" href="Frame.html#5153" class="Function Operator">⊓[</a> <a id="7307" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="7309" href="Frame.html#5153" class="Function Operator">]-greatest</a> <a id="7320" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7321" href="PatchFrame.html#7261" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="7323" href="PatchFrame.html#7296" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7324" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7326" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7327" href="PatchFrame.html#7269" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7329" href="PatchFrame.html#7296" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7330" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7332" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7333" href="PatchFrame.html#7277" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="7335" href="PatchFrame.html#7296" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7336" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7338" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7339" href="PatchFrame.html#7285" class="Bound">l⊑j</a> <a id="7343" href="PatchFrame.html#7296" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7344" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7346" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7347" href="PatchFrame.html#7291" class="Bound">l⊑k</a> <a id="7351" href="PatchFrame.html#7296" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7352" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
The meet of two Scott-continuous nuclei is itself Scott-continuous:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="⊓n-sc"></a><a id="7436" href="PatchFrame.html#7436" class="Function">⊓n-sc</a> <a id="7442" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7444" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7445" href="PatchFrame.html#7445" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="7447" href="PatchFrame.html#7447" class="Bound">𝓀</a> <a id="7449" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7451" href="Nucleus.html#601" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="7459" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a><a id="7460" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7462" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7464" href="PatchFrame.html#1342" class="Function">isScottCont</a> <a id="7476" href="PatchFrame.html#7445" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="7478" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7480" href="PatchFrame.html#1342" class="Function">isScottCont</a> <a id="7492" href="PatchFrame.html#7447" class="Bound">𝓀</a> <a id="7494" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7496" href="PatchFrame.html#1342" class="Function">isScottCont</a> <a id="7508" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7509" href="PatchFrame.html#7445" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="7511" href="PatchFrame.html#5273" class="Function Operator">⊓n</a> <a id="7514" href="PatchFrame.html#7447" class="Bound">𝓀</a><a id="7515" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="7517" href="PatchFrame.html#7436" class="Function">⊓n-sc</a> <a id="7523" href="PatchFrame.html#7523" class="Bound">𝒿</a><a id="7524" class="Symbol">@(</a><a id="7526" href="PatchFrame.html#7526" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="7528" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7530" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="7533" href="PatchFrame.html#7533" class="Bound">𝓀</a><a id="7534" class="Symbol">@(</a><a id="7536" href="PatchFrame.html#7536" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7538" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7540" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="7543" href="PatchFrame.html#7543" class="Bound">j-sc</a> <a id="7548" href="PatchFrame.html#7548" class="Bound">k-sc</a> <a id="7553" href="PatchFrame.html#7553" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="7555" href="PatchFrame.html#7555" class="Bound">U-dir</a><a id="7560" class="Symbol">@(_</a> <a id="7564" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7566" href="PatchFrame.html#7566" class="Bound">U-up</a><a id="7570" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7572" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="7576" href="PatchFrame.html#7526" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="7578" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7579" href="PatchFrame.html#1057" class="Function Operator">⋁</a> <a id="7581" href="PatchFrame.html#7553" class="Bound">U</a><a id="7582" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7584" href="PatchFrame.html#1006" class="Function Operator">⊓</a> <a id="7586" href="PatchFrame.html#7536" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7588" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7589" href="PatchFrame.html#1057" class="Function Operator">⋁</a> <a id="7591" href="PatchFrame.html#7553" class="Bound">U</a><a id="7592" class="Symbol">)</a>                                             <a id="7638" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#6490" class="Function Operator">≡⟨</a> <a id="7641" href="PatchFrame.html#8487" class="Function">⦅𝟏⦆</a> <a id="7645" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#6490" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>

  <a id="8530" href="PatchFrame.html#8530" class="Function">⦅𝟐⦆</a>  <a id="8535" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8537" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#1138" class="Function">cong</a> <a id="8542" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="8545" href="PatchFrame.html#8545" class="Bound">-</a> <a id="8547" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8549" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="8551" href="PatchFrame.html#1006" class="Function Operator">⊓</a> <a id="8553" href="PatchFrame.html#8545" class="Bound">-</a><a id="8554" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8556" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8557" href="PatchFrame.html#7548" class="Bound">k-sc</a> <a id="8562" href="PatchFrame.html#7553" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="8564" href="PatchFrame.html#7555" class="Bound">U-dir</a><a id="8569" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="8626" href="PatchFrame.html#8626" class="Function">⦅𝟒⦆</a>  <a id="8631" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8633" href="Poset.html#3283" class="Function Operator">⊑[</a> <a id="8636" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="8640" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="8642" href="Poset.html#3283" class="Function Operator">]-antisym</a> <a id="8652" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="8654" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="8656" href="PatchFrame.html#8378" class="Function">⦅𝟒a⦆</a> <a id="8661" href="PatchFrame.html#8409" class="Function">⦅𝟒b⦆</a>
</pre>
Using all these, we define the meet of two Scott-continuous nuclei.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="_⊓sc_"></a><a id="8748" href="PatchFrame.html#8748" class="Function Operator">_⊓sc_</a> <a id="8754" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8756" href="PatchFrame.html#1792" class="Function">ScottContNucleus</a> <a id="8773" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8775" href="PatchFrame.html#1792" class="Function">ScottContNucleus</a> <a id="8792" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8794" href="PatchFrame.html#1792" class="Function">ScottContNucleus</a>
<a id="8811" href="PatchFrame.html#8748" class="Function Operator">_⊓sc_</a> <a id="8817" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8818" href="PatchFrame.html#8818" class="Bound">𝒿</a><a id="8819" class="Symbol">@(</a><a id="8821" href="PatchFrame.html#8821" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="8823" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8825" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="8828" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8830" href="PatchFrame.html#8830" class="Bound">j-sc</a><a id="8834" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8836" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8837" href="PatchFrame.html#8837" class="Bound">𝓀</a><a id="8838" class="Symbol">@(</a><a id="8840" href="PatchFrame.html#8840" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8842" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8844" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="8847" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8849" href="PatchFrame.html#8849" class="Bound">k-sc</a><a id="8853" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8855" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8857" href="PatchFrame.html#8818" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="8859" href="PatchFrame.html#5273" class="Function Operator">⊓n</a> <a id="8862" href="PatchFrame.html#8837" class="Bound">𝓀</a> <a id="8864" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8866" href="PatchFrame.html#7436" class="Function">⊓n-sc</a> <a id="8872" href="PatchFrame.html#8818" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="8874" href="PatchFrame.html#8837" class="Bound">𝓀</a> <a id="8876" href="PatchFrame.html#8830" class="Bound">j-sc</a> <a id="8881" href="PatchFrame.html#8849" class="Bound">k-sc</a>
</pre>
which we verify to be a GLB operator as expected:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="⊓sc-meet"></a><a id="8950" href="PatchFrame.html#8950" class="Function">⊓sc-meet</a> <a id="8959" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8961" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="8963" href="Frame.html#1300" class="Function">isGLB</a> <a id="8969" href="PatchFrame.html#3822" class="Function">𝔖</a> <a id="8971" href="PatchFrame.html#8748" class="Function Operator">_⊓sc_</a> <a id="8977" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">]</a>
<a id="8979" href="PatchFrame.html#549" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="8983" href="PatchFrame.html#8950" class="Function">⊓sc-meet</a> <a id="8992" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8993" href="PatchFrame.html#8993" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="8995" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8997" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="9000" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9001" href="PatchFrame.html#9001" class="Bound">𝓀</a> <a id="9003" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="9005" class="Symbol">_)</a>          <a id="9017" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9019" href="PatchFrame.html#549" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="9023" href="PatchFrame.html#6929" class="Function">⊓n-meet</a> <a id="9031" href="PatchFrame.html#8993" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="9033" href="PatchFrame.html#9001" class="Bound">𝓀</a>
<a id="9035" href="PatchFrame.html#560" class="Field">snd</a> <a id="9039" href="PatchFrame.html#8950" class="Function">⊓sc-meet</a> <a id="9048" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9049" href="PatchFrame.html#9049" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="9051" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="9053" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="9056" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9057" href="PatchFrame.html#9057" class="Bound">𝓀</a> <a id="9059" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="9061" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="9064" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9065" href="PatchFrame.html#9065" class="Bound">𝓀′</a> <a id="9068" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="9070" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="9073" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9075" href="PatchFrame.html#560" class="Field">snd</a> <a id="9079" href="PatchFrame.html#6929" class="Function">⊓n-meet</a> <a id="9087" href="PatchFrame.html#9049" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="9089" href="PatchFrame.html#9057" class="Bound">𝓀</a> <a id="9091" href="PatchFrame.html#9065" class="Bound">𝓀′</a>
</pre>
Arbitrary join of nuclei
------------------------

This is the non-trivial part of this development.

### Directification of a family of nuclei

We first define following function `ℜ` such that, given a family `U ≔ { fᵢ : A →
A ∣ i ∈ I }` of endofunctions, and a list `i₀, …, iₙ` of indices from `I`, `ℜ U
[i₀, …, iₙ]` denotes the composition `fᵢₙ ∘ ⋯ ∘ fᵢ₀`.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="ℜ"></a><a id="9468" href="PatchFrame.html#9468" class="Function">ℜ</a> <a id="9470" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9472" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9473" href="PatchFrame.html#9473" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9475" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9477" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#1230" class="Primitive">Type</a> <a id="9482" href="Basis.html#2593" class="Generalizable">ℓ</a><a id="9483" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9485" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9487" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9488" href="PatchFrame.html#9488" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="9490" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9492" href="Basis.html#5634" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="9496" href="Basis.html#2595" class="Generalizable">ℓ′</a> <a id="9499" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9500" href="PatchFrame.html#9473" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9502" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9504" href="PatchFrame.html#9473" class="Bound">A</a><a id="9505" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="9508" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9510" href="Agda.Builtin.List.html#148" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="9515" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9516" href="Basis.html#5709" class="Function">index</a> <a id="9522" href="PatchFrame.html#9488" class="Bound">α</a><a id="9523" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9525" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9527" href="PatchFrame.html#9473" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9529" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9531" href="PatchFrame.html#9473" class="Bound">A</a>
<a id="9533" href="PatchFrame.html#9468" class="Function">ℜ</a> <a id="9535" href="PatchFrame.html#9535" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="9537" href="Agda.Builtin.List.html#185" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a>       <a id="9546" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9548" href="Cubical.Foundations.Function.html#344" class="Function">idfun</a> <a id="9554" class="Symbol">_</a>
<a id="9556" href="PatchFrame.html#9468" class="Function">ℜ</a> <a id="9558" href="PatchFrame.html#9558" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="9560" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9561" href="PatchFrame.html#9561" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="9563" href="Agda.Builtin.List.html#200" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="9565" href="PatchFrame.html#9565" class="Bound">is</a><a id="9567" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9569" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9571" href="PatchFrame.html#9468" class="Function">ℜ</a> <a id="9573" href="PatchFrame.html#9558" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="9575" href="PatchFrame.html#9565" class="Bound">is</a> <a id="9578" href="Cubical.Foundations.Function.html#402" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="9580" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9581" href="PatchFrame.html#9558" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="9583" href="Basis.html#5802" class="Function Operator">$</a> <a id="9585" href="PatchFrame.html#9561" class="Bound">i</a><a id="9586" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
Using `ℜ`, we define the family obtained from such a family of endofunctions
that consists of all such compositions.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="ℜ-fam"></a><a id="9719" href="PatchFrame.html#9719" class="Function">ℜ-fam</a> <a id="9725" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9727" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9728" href="PatchFrame.html#9728" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9730" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9732" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#1230" class="Primitive">Type</a> <a id="9737" href="PatchFrame.html#758" class="Bound">𝒰</a><a id="9738" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9740" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9741" href="PatchFrame.html#9741" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="9743" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9745" href="Basis.html#5634" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="9749" href="PatchFrame.html#762" class="Bound">𝒲</a> <a id="9751" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9752" href="PatchFrame.html#9728" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9754" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9756" href="PatchFrame.html#9728" class="Bound">A</a><a id="9757" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="9760" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9762" href="Basis.html#5634" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="9766" href="PatchFrame.html#762" class="Bound">𝒲</a> <a id="9768" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9769" href="PatchFrame.html#9728" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9771" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9773" href="PatchFrame.html#9728" class="Bound">A</a><a id="9774" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="9776" href="PatchFrame.html#9719" class="Function">ℜ-fam</a> <a id="9782" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9783" class="Argument">A</a> <a id="9785" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9787" href="PatchFrame.html#9787" class="Bound">A</a><a id="9788" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9790" href="PatchFrame.html#9790" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="9792" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9794" href="Agda.Builtin.List.html#148" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="9799" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9800" href="Basis.html#5709" class="Function">index</a> <a id="9806" href="PatchFrame.html#9790" class="Bound">α</a><a id="9807" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9809" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="9811" href="PatchFrame.html#9468" class="Function">ℜ</a> <a id="9813" href="PatchFrame.html#9790" class="Bound">α</a>
</pre>
We will use this function to compute the join of a family of nuclei. The key
idea is that the family of compositions is a directed family even if the family
we start with is not.

Notice that the identity function is always a (pre)nucleus.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="id-is-nuclear"></a><a id="10069" href="PatchFrame.html#10069" class="Function">id-is-nuclear</a> <a id="10083" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10085" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10086" href="PatchFrame.html#10086" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="10088" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10090" href="Frame.html#3701" class="Function">Frame</a> <a id="10096" href="Basis.html#2598" class="Generalizable">ℓ₀</a> <a id="10099" href="Basis.html#2601" class="Generalizable">ℓ₁</a> <a id="10102" href="PatchFrame.html#762" class="Bound">𝒲</a><a id="10103" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10105" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10107" href="Prenucleus.html#493" class="Function">isPrenuclear</a> <a id="10120" href="PatchFrame.html#10086" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="10122" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10123" href="Cubical.Foundations.Function.html#344" class="Function">idfun</a> <a id="10129" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="10131" href="PatchFrame.html#10086" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="10133" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a><a id="10135" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="10137" href="PatchFrame.html#10069" class="Function">id-is-nuclear</a> <a id="10151" href="PatchFrame.html#10151" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="10153" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10155" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="10158" href="PatchFrame.html#10158" class="Bound">_</a> <a id="10160" href="PatchFrame.html#10160" class="Bound">_</a> <a id="10162" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10164" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#898" class="Function">refl</a><a id="10168" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10170" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10172" href="Poset.html#3014" class="Function Operator">⊑[</a> <a id="10175" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="10179" href="PatchFrame.html#10151" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="10181" href="Poset.html#3014" class="Function Operator">]-refl</a>
</pre>
Compositions of prenuclei are prenuclei meaning given a family of nuclei, its
`ℜ-fam` is a family of prenuclei

<pre class="Agda"><a id="ℜ-fam-prenucleus"></a><a id="10313" href="PatchFrame.html#10313" class="Function">ℜ-fam-prenucleus</a> <a id="10330" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10332" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10333" href="PatchFrame.html#10333" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="10335" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10337" href="Basis.html#5634" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="10341" href="PatchFrame.html#762" class="Bound">𝒲</a> <a id="10343" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10344" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="10346" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="10348" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="10351" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10353" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="10355" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="10357" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a><a id="10359" class="Symbol">))</a>
                 <a id="10379" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10381" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="10383" href="PatchFrame.html#10383" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="10385" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10387" href="Basis.html#5709" class="Function">index</a> <a id="10393" href="PatchFrame.html#10333" class="Bound">K</a><a id="10394" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10396" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10398" href="Prenucleus.html#493" class="Function">isPrenuclear</a> <a id="10411" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="10413" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10414" href="PatchFrame.html#10333" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="10416" href="Basis.html#5802" class="Function Operator">$</a> <a id="10418" href="PatchFrame.html#10383" class="Bound">i</a><a id="10419" class="Symbol">))</a>
                 <a id="10439" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10441" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10442" href="PatchFrame.html#10442" class="Bound">is</a> <a id="10445" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10447" href="Agda.Builtin.List.html#148" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="10452" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10453" href="Basis.html#5709" class="Function">index</a> <a id="10459" href="PatchFrame.html#10333" class="Bound">K</a><a id="10460" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="10463" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10465" href="Prenucleus.html#493" class="Function">isPrenuclear</a> <a id="10478" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="10480" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10481" href="PatchFrame.html#9719" class="Function">ℜ-fam</a> <a id="10487" href="PatchFrame.html#10333" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="10489" href="Basis.html#5802" class="Function Operator">$</a> <a id="10491" href="PatchFrame.html#10442" class="Bound">is</a><a id="10493" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="10495" href="PatchFrame.html#10313" class="Function">ℜ-fam-prenucleus</a> <a id="10512" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="10514" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="10516" href="Agda.Builtin.List.html#185" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a>       <a id="10525" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10527" href="PatchFrame.html#10069" class="Function">id-is-nuclear</a> <a id="10541" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a>
<a id="10543" href="PatchFrame.html#10313" class="Function">ℜ-fam-prenucleus</a> <a id="10560" href="PatchFrame.html#10560" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="10562" href="PatchFrame.html#10562" class="Bound">φ</a> <a id="10564" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10565" href="PatchFrame.html#10565" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="10567" href="Agda.Builtin.List.html#200" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="10569" href="PatchFrame.html#10569" class="Bound">is</a><a id="10571" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10573" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10575" href="PatchFrame.html#10846" class="Function">n₀</a> <a id="10578" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10580" href="PatchFrame.html#11187" class="Function">n₁</a>

  <a id="10663" href="PatchFrame.html#10663" class="Function">ih</a> <a id="10666" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10668" href="Prenucleus.html#493" class="Function">isPrenuclear</a> <a id="10681" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="10683" href="PatchFrame.html#10619" class="Function">j′</a>

  <a id="10959" href="PatchFrame.html#10846" class="Function">n₀</a> <a id="10962" href="PatchFrame.html#10962" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="10964" href="PatchFrame.html#10964" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="10966" class="Symbol">=</a>

</pre>
For convenience, we introduce the following notation: given a some family
`J` of nuclei, `J ^*` denotes its `ℜ-fam`.

`J ^*` is always inhabited.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="J*-inhabited"></a><a id="12276" href="PatchFrame.html#12276" class="Function">J*-inhabited</a> <a id="12289" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12291" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12292" href="PatchFrame.html#12292" class="Bound">J</a> <a id="12294" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12296" href="Basis.html#5634" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="12300" href="PatchFrame.html#762" class="Bound">𝒲</a> <a id="12302" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12303" href="Nucleus.html#601" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="12311" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a><a id="12312" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="12315" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12317" href="Basis.html#7710" class="Datatype Operator">∥</a> <a id="12319" href="Basis.html#5709" class="Function">index</a> <a id="12325" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12326" href="PatchFrame.html#12292" class="Bound">J</a> <a id="12328" href="PatchFrame.html#11427" class="Function Operator">^*</a><a id="12330" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12332" href="Basis.html#7710" class="Datatype Operator">∥</a>

</pre>
Some nice notation for applying a certain nucleus in a family to an argument.

</pre>
Given a family `J` of Scott-continuous nuclei, everything in `J ^*` is
Scott-continuous.

### A lemma

<pre class="Agda"><a id="joins-commute"></a><a id="15156" href="PatchFrame.html#15156" class="Function">joins-commute</a> <a id="15170" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15172" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15173" href="PatchFrame.html#15173" class="Bound">J</a> <a id="15175" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15177" href="Basis.html#5634" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="15181" href="PatchFrame.html#762" class="Bound">𝒲</a> <a id="15183" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15184" href="Nucleus.html#601" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="15192" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a><a id="15193" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="15196" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15197" href="PatchFrame.html#15197" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="15199" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15201" href="Basis.html#5634" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="15205" href="PatchFrame.html#762" class="Bound">𝒲</a> <a id="15207" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="15209" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="15211" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a><a id="15213" class="Symbol">)</a>

Some shorthand notation that we will use when defining the join.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="𝕚"></a><a id="16078" href="PatchFrame.html#16078" class="Function">𝕚</a> <a id="16080" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16082" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16083" href="PatchFrame.html#16083" class="Bound">J</a> <a id="16085" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16087" href="Basis.html#5634" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="16091" href="PatchFrame.html#762" class="Bound">𝒲</a> <a id="16093" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16094" href="Nucleus.html#601" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="16102" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a><a id="16103" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="16106" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16108" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="16110" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="16112" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a> <a id="16115" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16117" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="16119" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="16121" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a>
<a id="16124" href="PatchFrame.html#16078" class="Function">𝕚</a> <a id="16126" href="PatchFrame.html#16126" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="16128" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16130" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="16132" href="PatchFrame.html#16132" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="16134" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16136" href="PatchFrame.html#1057" class="Function Operator">⋁</a> <a id="16138" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">⁅</a> <a id="16140" href="PatchFrame.html#16146" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="16142" href="PatchFrame.html#16132" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="16144" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">∣</a> <a id="16146" href="PatchFrame.html#16146" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="16148" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">ε</a> <a id="16150" href="PatchFrame.html#16126" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="16152" href="PatchFrame.html#11427" class="Function Operator">^*</a> <a id="16155" href="Basis.html#6216" class="Function">⁆</a>
</pre>
### The definition of the join

      <a id="21278" class="Keyword">where</a>
      <a id="21290" href="PatchFrame.html#21290" class="Function">ih</a> <a id="21293" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="21295" href="PatchFrame.html#20881" class="Function">lemma</a> <a id="21301" href="PatchFrame.html#20992" class="Bound">is</a> <a id="21304" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21305" href="PatchFrame.html#20505" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="21307" href="PatchFrame.html#20996" class="Bound">x</a><a id="21308" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
Distributivity
--------------

We construct a rather involved proof of the fact that binary meets distribute
over arbitrary joins.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="dupl"></a><a id="21455" href="PatchFrame.html#21455" class="Function">dupl</a> <a id="21460" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21462" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21463" href="PatchFrame.html#21463" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="21465" href="PatchFrame.html#21465" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="21467" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21469" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="21471" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="21473" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">∣F</a><a id="21475" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21477" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21479" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="21481" href="PatchFrame.html#21463" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="21483" href="PatchFrame.html#1006" class="Function Operator">⊓</a> <a id="21485" href="PatchFrame.html#21465" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="21487" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">⊑[</a> <a id="21490" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="21494" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="21496" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">]</a> <a id="21498" href="PatchFrame.html#21463" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="21500" href="PatchFrame.html#1006" class="Function Operator">⊓</a> <a id="21502" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21503" href="PatchFrame.html#21463" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="21505" href="PatchFrame.html#1006" class="Function Operator">⊓</a> <a id="21507" href="PatchFrame.html#21465" class="Bound">y</a><a id="21508" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21510" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">]</a>
<a id="21512" href="PatchFrame.html#21455" class="Function">dupl</a> <a id="21517" href="PatchFrame.html#21517" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="21519" href="PatchFrame.html#21519" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="21521" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="21523" href="Frame.html#5153" class="Function Operator">⊓[</a> <a id="21526" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="21528" href="Frame.html#5153" class="Function Operator">]-greatest</a> <a id="21539" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="21541" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="21543" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="21545" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21546" href="Frame.html#4893" class="Function Operator">⊓[</a> <a id="21549" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="21551" href="Frame.html#4893" class="Function Operator">]-lower₀</a> <a id="21560" href="PatchFrame.html#21517" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="21562" href="PatchFrame.html#21519" class="Bound">y</a><a id="21563" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21565" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21566" href="Poset.html#3014" class="Function Operator">⊑[</a> <a id="21569" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="21573" href="PatchFrame.html#748" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="21575" href="Poset.html#3014" class="Function Operator">]-refl</a> <a id="21582" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21583" href="PatchFrame.html#21517" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="21585" href="PatchFrame.html#1006" class="Function Operator">⊓</a> <a id="21587" href="PatchFrame.html#21519" class="Bound">y</a><a id="21588" class="Symbol">))</a>

The definition of the frame
---------------------------
